# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

Perfect! I've completed a comprehensive analysis of the hot restart mechanism in envoyproxy/envoy and created the answer file. 

## Summary

I've identified **34 C++ source files** that implement the hot restart mechanism across these key components:

### **Core Components:**
1. **HotRestart Interface** - Main API in `envoy/server/hot_restart.h`
2. **HotRestartImpl** - Main implementation coordinating parent/child processes
3. **HotRestartingParent** & **HotRestartingChild** - Parent and child sides of the protocol
4. **HotRestartingBase** & **RpcStream** - Unix domain socket communication infrastructure
5. **DrainManagerImpl** - Graceful connection draining sequence
6. **StatMerger** - Parent statistics merging into child
7. **SharedMemory** - Inter-process synchronization via mmap

### **Key Features Covered:**
- ✅ **Parent/child process handshake** - Unix domain socket negotiation
- ✅ **Socket passing** - File descriptor passing via `sendmsg()`/`recvmsg()`
- ✅ **Drain sequence** - Graceful draining with configurable timeouts
- ✅ **Child readiness signaling** - `drainParentListeners()` and drain callbacks
- ✅ **UDP forwarding** - Special handling for QUIC packets during drain
- ✅ **Statistics merging** - Parent stats imported into child

The answer file at `/workspace/answer.json` contains the complete list of files, key symbols, important method chains, and a detailed narrative explaining how all components work together to achieve zero-downtime Envoy binary updates.

components:\\n\\n## Core Interface and Implementation\\n\\nThe **HotRestart interface** is defined in `envoy/server/hot_restart.h` and provides the public API for hot restart operations. The main implementation is **HotRestartImpl** in `source/server/hot_restart_impl.h` and `source/server/hot_restart_impl.cc`, which coordinates parent and child process communication using shared memory and Unix domain sockets.\\n\\n## Parent/Child Process Handshake\\n\\n**HotRestartingParent** (`source/server/hot_restarting_parent.h/.cc`) handles the parent process side of the hot restart protocol:\\n- Binds to Unix domain sockets and listens for requests from child processes\\n- Exports listener sockets to the child via file descriptor passing (using `sendmsg`/`recvmsg`)\\n- Drains listeners when the child is ready to take over\\n- Exports parent statistics to the child for merging\\n\\n**HotRestartingChild** (`source/server/hot_restarting_child.h/.cc`) handles the child process side:\\n- Connects to parent's Unix domain sockets to request resources\\n- Requests listener socket duplication from the parent\\n- Signals parent when ready to receive connections\\n- Handles parent drained callbacks for UDP listener forwarding\\n\\n## Socket Communication Infrastructure\\n\\n**HotRestartingBase** (`source/server/hot_restarting_base.h/.cc`) provides shared base functionality including the **RpcStream** class, which implements:\\n- Unix domain socket creation and binding using `AF_UNIX, SOCK_DGRAM`\\n- Message sending via `sendmsg()` to pass file descriptors across process boundaries\\n- Message receiving via `recvmsg()` to handle control data with file descriptors\\n- Both main RPC stream and UDP forwarding stream support\\n\\nThe socket communication uses Protocol Buffers defined in `source/server/hot_restart.proto` with **HotRestartMessage** types for child->parent requests and parent->child replies.\\n\\n## Drain Sequence Implementation\\n\\n**DrainManagerImpl** (`source/server/drain_manager_impl.h/.cc`) implements the drain sequence:\\n- Tracks draining state per connection direction (inbound/all)\\n- Creates child drain managers that cascade drain status from parent to child\\n- Manages drain completion callbacks and timeouts\\n- Supports gradual vs. immediate drain strategies\\n- Integrates with listeners to gracefully close connections during hot restart\\n\\n## Shared Memory and Initialization\\n\\n**SharedMemory** structure in `source/server/hot_restart_impl.h` contains:\\n- Synchronization primitives for parent/child coordination\\n- Initialization flags (SHMEM_FLAGS_INITIALIZING)\\n- Memory tracking for hot restart version compatibility\\n- Atomic flags managed via `mmap()` of a named shared memory region\\n\\n## Statistics Merging\\n\\n**StatMerger** (`source/common/stats/stat_merger.h/.cc`) handles merging parent statistics into the child:\\n- Exports gauges and counters from parent process\\n- Child imports and accumulates parent statistics\\n- Handles special stat names like hot_restart_generation\\n\\n## OS System Calls Layer\\n\\n**HotRestartOsSysCalls** (`envoy/api/os_sys_calls_hot_restart.h`) and its POSIX implementation **HotRestartOsSysCallsImpl** (`source/common/api/posix/os_sys_calls_impl_hot_restart.h/.cc`) provide abstracted access to:\\n- Shared memory operations (`shm_open`)\\n- Low-level system calls for the hot restart mechanism\\n\\n## UDP Listener Forwarding\\n\\nSpecialized UDP forwarding support in `source/server/hot_restarting_base.h` includes:\\n- Separate UDP forwarding RPC stream for QUIC packet forwarding\\n- UdpForwardingContext for managing QUIC connections during drain\\n- Listener worker routing for proper packet delivery\\n\\n## Child Process Readiness Signaling\\n\\nChild readiness is signaled through:\\n- **drainParentListeners()** call indicating child is initialized and ready for traffic\\n- **registerParentDrainedCallback()** for listeners to register callbacks when parent drains\\n- **allDrainsImplicitlyComplete()** signaling drain completion\\n- **abortDueToFailedParentConnection()** handling parent connection failures\\n\\n## Integration Points\\n\\n- **Options handling** in `source/server/options_impl.h/.cc` for command-line arguments (--base-id, --restart-epoch, --hot-restart-version, etc.)\\n- **Server integration** in `source/exe/stripped_main_base.cc` and `source/exe/main_common.cc` for creating and initializing components:\\n\\n## Core Interface and Implementation\\n\\nThe **HotRestart interface** is defined in `envoy/server/hot_restart.h` and provides the public API for hot restart operations. The main implementation is **HotRestartImpl** in `source/server/hot_restart_impl.h` and `source/server/hot_restart_impl.cc`, which coordinates parent and child process communication using shared memory and Unix domain sockets.\\n\\n## Parent/Child Process Handshake\\n\\n**HotRestartingParent** (`source/server/hot_restarting_parent.h/.cc`) handles the parent process side of the hot restart protocol:\\n- Binds to Unix domain sockets and listens for requests from child processes\\n- Exports listener sockets to the child via file descriptor passing (using `sendmsg`/`recvmsg`)\\n- Drains listeners when the child is ready to take over\\n- Exports parent statistics to the child for merging\\n\\n**HotRestartingChild** (`source/server/hot_restarting_child.h/.cc`) handles the child process side:\\n- Connects to parent's Unix domain sockets to request resources\\n- Requests listener socket duplication from the parent\\n- Signals parent when ready to receive connections\\n- Handles parent drained callbacks for UDP listener forwarding\\n\\n## Socket Communication Infrastructure\\n\\n**HotRestartingBase** (`source/server/hot_restarting_base.h/.cc`) provides shared base functionality including the **RpcStream** class, which implements:\\n- Unix domain socket creation and binding using `AF_UNIX, SOCK_DGRAM`\\n- Message sending via `sendmsg()` to pass file descriptors across process boundaries\\n- Message receiving via `recvmsg()` to handle control data with file descriptors\\n- Both main RPC stream and UDP forwarding stream support\\n\\nThe socket communication uses Protocol Buffers defined in `source/server/hot_restart.proto` with **HotRestartMessage** types for child->parent requests and parent->child replies.\\n\\n## Drain Sequence Implementation\\n\\n**DrainManagerImpl** (`source/server/drain_manager_impl.h/.cc`) implements the drain sequence:\\n- Tracks draining state per connection direction (inbound/all)\\n- Creates child drain managers that cascade drain status from parent to child\\n- Manages drain completion callbacks and timeouts\\n- Supports gradual vs. immediate drain strategies\\n- Integrates with listeners to gracefully close connections during hot restart\\n\\n## Shared Memory and Initialization\\n\\n**SharedMemory** structure in `source/server/hot_restart_impl.h` contains:\\n- Synchronization primitives for parent/child coordination\\n- Initialization flags (SHMEM_FLAGS_INITIALIZING)\\n- Memory tracking for hot restart version compatibility\\n- Atomic flags managed via `mmap()` of a named shared memory region\\n\\n## Statistics Merging\\n\\n**StatMerger** (`source/common/stats/stat_merger.h/.cc`) handles merging parent statistics into the child:\\n- Exports gauges and counters from parent process\\n- Child imports and accumulates parent statistics\\n- Handles special stat names like hot_restart_generation\\n\\n## OS System Calls Layer\\n\\n**HotRestartOsSysCalls** (`envoy/api/os_sys_calls_hot_restart.h`) and its POSIX implementation **HotRestartOsSysCallsImpl** (`source/common/api/posix/os_sys_calls_impl_hot_restart.h/.cc`) provide abstracted access to:\\n- Shared memory operations (`shm_open`)\\n- Low-level system calls for the hot restart mechanism\\n\\n## UDP Listener Forwarding\\n\\nSpecialized UDP forwarding support in `source/server/hot_restarting_base.h` includes:\\n- Separate UDP forwarding RPC stream for QUIC packet forwarding\\n- UdpForwardingContext for managing QUIC connections during drain\\n- Listener worker routing for proper packet delivery\\n\\n## Child Process Readiness Signaling\\n\\nChild readiness is signaled through:\\n- **drainParentListeners()** call indicating child is initialized and ready for traffic\\n- **registerParentDrainedCallback()** for listeners to register callbacks when parent drains\\n- **allDrainsImplicitlyComplete()** signaling drain completion\\n- **abortDueToFailedParentConnection()** handling parent connection failures\\n\\n## Integration Points\\n\\n- **Options handling** in `source/server/options_impl.h/.cc` for command-line arguments (--base-id, --restart-epoch, --hot-restart-version, etc.)\\n- **Server integration** in `source/exe/stripped_main_base.cc` and `source/exe/main_common.cc` for creating and initializing HotRestartImpl\\n- **Listener management** integration for socket duplication and drain coordination\\n- **Stats export** integration with server statistics stores\\n\\n## Testing\\n\\nComprehensive Integration tests of full hot restart flow\\n\\nThe implementation handles the complete hot restart lifecycle: parent process initialization, child process startup and handshaking, listener socket passing, connection draining, statistics merging, and graceful parent shutdown.\"\n}\n",
